# Format of this file: 
#	A target function in a matrix format is followed by a sample implementation by the proposed system.
#	The implementation shows operators in the same stage within curly brackets ({}) and 
#		the qubit numbers where operators are applied in square brackets ([]). 
#	For example, {'H':[[0],[1]], 'CNOT':[[2,3]]} indicates a stage with 
#		(i) two H operators on qubits 0 and 1 and 
#		(ii) one CNOT operator on qubits 2 and 3.
#	Operators Tct and Sct are conjugate transposes of T and S, respectively.
